window.listingIcon = function(listing) {
  var type = listing.type || listing._type
  if (type == 'dispensary' && listing.is_delivery == true) {
    type = 'delivery'
  } else if (type == 'delivery' && listing.is_delivery == false) {
    type = 'dispensary'
  }
  if (listing.license_type === 'recreational') {
    var icon = (type === 'dispensary' && listing.package_level_raw !== 0) ? 'rec_' : '';
  } else if (listing.license_type === 'hybrid') {
    var icon = (type === 'dispensary' && listing.package_level_raw !== 0) ? 'hybrid_' : '';
  } else {
    var icon = '';
  }

  icon += type;

  icon += (function() {
    switch (parseInt(listing.feature_order)) {
      case 1:
        return '_gold_marker';
      case 2:
        return '_silver_marker';
      case 3:
        return '_bronze_marker';
      default:
        switch (parseInt(listing.package_level_raw)) {
          case 0:
            return '_free_marker';
          default:
            return '_plus_marker';
        }
    }
  })();

  return icon;
};
